Descriptive statistics

For completeness, the following table of counts for each cohort and ethnicity, organized by census linkage group

Census linkage sets are denoted in these figures by the last two digits of the latest census and the last two digits of the first census in the linkage set. E.g., “0601” indicates the linkage was from 2006 back to 2001.

For repeated measures Year column indicates which year the measure if for.
